## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x00AF [0x1A] CALL_SUBROUTINE(address=0x161C)
  1: 0x00B2 [0x02] IF !(ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[8] == 12*) GOTO 0x00C9
  2: 0x00BA [0x6E] EventEntity uses emote 8*
  3: 0x00C1 [0x99] Wait for EventEntity animation to complete
  4: 0x00C6 [0x01] GOTO 0x00D5

SUBROUTINE_00C9:
  5: 0x00C9 [0x6E] EventEntity uses emote 7*
  6: 0x00D0 [0x99] Wait for EventEntity animation to complete
  7: 0x00D5 [0x1C] WAIT(180* ticks)
  8: 0x00D8 [0x32] ExtData[1]->MainSpeed = 13* * 0.1
  9: 0x00DB [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: EventEntity moves to X=351.390*, Z=-230.323*, Y=7.821*
 10: 0x00E3 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: Update entity position (mode=1)
 11: 0x00E5 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()

 12: 0x161C [0x41] GET_BIT_WORK_RANGE(start_bit=10*, end_bit=13*, source=Work_Zone[9], result=ExtData[1]->WorkLocal[8])
 13: 0x1625 [0x1B] RETURN
```
